<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wercman</i>. ***werpen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:werpen.html>werpen</a> (5657)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:werpen.html>werpen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">werpan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*werpaną</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:werpen.html>werpen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to throw</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of animals</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give birth</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wesp.html>wesp</a> (31445)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier Modern Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wespe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wespe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wespa</i>, with metathesis from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wepsō-</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wobʰseh₂</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wasp</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*webʰ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">weave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wespe</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Wösp</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wasp</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">wasp</span>, used certain members of the order Hymenoptera, especially of the superfamily Vespoidea</li></ol>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wesp.html>wesp</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">nest</i>.

***weten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:weten.html>weten</a> (139)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wēten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">witan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*witaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wóyde</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">know</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a root <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> from the root <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weyd-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weten.html>weten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to know (knowledge)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>weet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:planeet.html>planeet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heet.html>heet</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>know</b> what that planet <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> called.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to remember
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>weet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:nog.html>nog</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:koud.html>koud</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vorig.html>vorig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I still <b>remember</b> how cold it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> last year.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">auxiliary<span class="ib-comma">,</span> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></i></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be able to, to manage to (literally, "to know how to/to know of a way to")
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> Frisii <a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> Germaans <a href = vnd.unilang:volk.html>volk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:net.html>net</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verscheidene.html>verscheidene</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:andere.html>andere</a> Germaanse <a href = vnd.unilang:volkeren.html>volkeren</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wisten.html>wisten</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:fel.html>fel</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:verdedigen.html>verdedigen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tegen.html>tegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Romeinen. <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>Toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moesten.html>moesten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Frisii <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jaar.html>jaar</a> 12 <a href = vnd.unilang:onderwerpen.html>onderwerpen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doordat.html>doordat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:veldheer.html>veldheer</a> Drusus <a href = vnd.unilang:hen.html>hen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wist.html>wist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:verslaan.html>verslaan</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The Frisii <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> a Germanic people and just like various other Germanic peoples they <b><a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> able to</b> fiercely defend themselves against the Romans. Nevertheless, the Frisii <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> to subject themselves in the year 12 because warlord Drusus <b><a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> able to</b> defeat them.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voornamelijk.html>voornamelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lokaal.html>lokaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niveau.html>niveau</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:succesvolle.html>succesvolle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:partij.html>partij</a> Freie Wähler <b><a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>weet</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eerst.html>eerst</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ergens.html>ergens</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> deelstaatniveau <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> kiesdrempel <b><a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:halen.html>halen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The party Freie Wähler, successful primarily at the local level, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> able</b> for the first time to achieve the election threshold somewhere at the state level.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***wetenschap.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wetenschap.html>wetenschap</a> (2500)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weten.html>weten</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-schap</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wetenschap.html>wetenschap</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wetenschappen.html>wetenschappen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> knowledge
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoe.html>Hoe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kan.html>kan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hieraan.html>hieraan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meedoen.html>meedoen</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wetenschap.html>wetenschap</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uiteindelijk.html>uiteindelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toch.html>toch</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">How can I participate in this in the <b>knowledge</b> that it will ultimately be for nought?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>science, scholarly knowledge, scholarship <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">collective discipline of learning acquired through any scholarly method; totality of knowledge</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>any academic discipline; in general, the sciences and humanities <a href = vnd.unilang:taken.html>taken</a> as a whole</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i><a href = vnd.unilang:wetenschap.html>Wetenschap</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> a much broader meaning than the English word <i><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">science</i></i>. The English word <i>science</i> refers to systematically acquired, objective knowledge obtained through a particular methodology (such as the scientific method), and includes only natural sciences, social sciences, and formal sciences.  In contrast, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wetenschap.html>wetenschap</a></i> also includes the humanities and philosophy and refers to learning and knowledge in general, whether obtained through scientific or non-scientific means.  For example, writing a scholarly book about an author's life and works <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wetenschap.html>wetenschap</a></i> but not "science".
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">boekwetenschap</span></li>

<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">geschiedswetenschap</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">history</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

***wetgever.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wetgever.html>wetgever</a> (34514)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wetgever.html>wetgever</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wetgeven</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to legislate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wetgever.html>wetgever</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wetgever.html>wetgevers</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl">wetgeveren</b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wetgever.html>wetgevertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

***wezen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wezen.html>wezen</a> (1563)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i>. The infinitive <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wezen.html>wezen</a></i> (from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wesaną</i>) <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the original infinitive of the verb but <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> fallen into marginal use, typically in an informal register or in dialects.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wezen.html>wezen</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wezens.html>wezens</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wezentje.html>wezentje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A being, creature</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">as the second part of a compound noun</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> system, sector, institution (in an abstract sense)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">used absolutely, with definite article or possessive determiner</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The essence of something
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>Zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vloek.html>vloek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:haar.html>haar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:diepste.html>diepste</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wezen.html>wezen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geraakt.html>geraakt</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">His curse <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> hit her in her deepest core.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***whiplash.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:whiplash.html>whiplash</a> (24322)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">whip</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lash</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> articles on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/whiplash" class="extiw" title="w:whiplash"><a href = vnd.unilang:whiplash.html>whiplash</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/whiplash" class="extiw" title="w:whiplash">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whiplash.html>whiplash</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">whiplashes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>the lash of a whip</li>
<li>an injury to the upper spine connected to a violent jerk of the head in either a backward or forward or side to side direction, resembling the motion of a whip
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whiplash.html>whiplash</a> injury</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">whiplash-associated disorder</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The exact causal chain leading to the medical condition as well as the objectivisation of its diagnostics are still controversial, thus the attributability of symptoms to the <a href = vnd.unilang:acts.html>acts</a> of tortfeasors <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> frequently subject to dispute.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whiplash.html>whiplash</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">whiplashes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">whiplashing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">whiplashed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To jerk back and forth; to buffet
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2008</b>,  December 23,  “Nicholas Confessore”, in  <cite>Resistance to Kennedy Grows among Democrats</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/2008/12/24/nyregion/24kennedy.html">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span> Ms. Kennedy <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> <b>whiplashed</b> by assertions that she <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> at once protected and presumptuous.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>To lash as if with a whip
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1990</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/V.C._Andrews" class="extiw" title="w:V.C. Andrews">V.C. Andrews</a>,  <cite>My Sweet Audrina</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?id=KH3v9OiekKcC">[2]</a></sup>, <small>→ISBN</small>, page 98:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">After a while, he let go of my hand in order to protect his own face from being <b>whiplashed</b> by the low <a href = vnd.unilang:branches.html>branches</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:whiplash.html>whiplash</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>  
</p>

***whist.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:whist.html>whist</a> (55403)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium. Particularly: “what does this have to do with silence”)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whist.html>whist</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">whists</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Any of several four-player card games, similar to bridge.</li>
<li>A session of playing this card game.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">German <a href = vnd.unilang:whist.html>whist</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">long <a href = vnd.unilang:whist.html>whist</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">Russian <a href = vnd.unilang:whist.html>whist</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">short <a href = vnd.unilang:whist.html>whist</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">solo <a href = vnd.unilang:whist.html>whist</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:whist.html>whist</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">silent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly onomatopoeic.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whist.html>whist</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Alternative spelling of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">whisht</i></span></span>. Silence!, quiet!, hush!, <a href = vnd.unilang:shhh.html>shhh</a>!, shush!
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1860</b>,  anonymous,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:heroes.html>Heroes</a> and Hunters of the West</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/dirs/2/6/9/6/26965/26965-h/26965-h.htm">[1]</a></sup>, HTML edition, The Gutenberg Project, published <i>2008</i>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">… for scarcely <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> they descended one hundred <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a>, when a low “<b><a href = vnd.unilang:whist.html>whist</a></b>” from the girl, warned them of present danger.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whist.html>whist</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">whists</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">whisting</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">whisted</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To hush, shush, or silence; to still.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Spenser to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To become silent.
<dl><dd><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> find and add a quotation of Surrey to this entry?)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whist.html>whist</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:whist.html>whist</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:whist.html>whist</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Silent, husht.
<ul><li><b>c. 1610-11</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Tempest" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Tempest">The Tempest</a></i>, Act I, Scene ii<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.opensourceshakespeare.org/views/plays/play_view.php?WorkID=tempestamp;Scope=entireamp;pleasewait=1amp;msg=pl">[2]</a></sup>:
<dl><dd>Come unto these yellow <a href = vnd.unilang:sands.html>sands</a>, / And then take hands: / Courtsied when you have and kiss'd / The wild waves <b><a href = vnd.unilang:whist.html>whist</a></b>, / Foot it featly here and there; / And, sweet sprites, the burthen bear.<span class="q-hellip-sp"> </span><span class="q-hellip-b">[</span>…<span class="q-hellip-b">]</span><span class="q-hellip-b"> </span></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***whit.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:whit.html>whit</a> (24321)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wiȝt</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wiht</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a>, person, creature, being, <a href = vnd.unilang:whit.html>whit</a>, thing, something, anything</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wihtą</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thing, creature</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wihtiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">essence, object</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wekti-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">cause, sake, thing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wekʷ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to say, tell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">wiht</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">creature, thing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicht.html>wicht</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicht.html>Wicht</a></i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wight.html>wight</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whit.html>whit</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">whits</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The smallest part or particle imaginable; an iota.
<dl><dd><i>He worked tirelessly to collect and wind a ball of string eight <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a> around, and it <a href = vnd.unilang:matters.html>matters</a> not one <b><a href = vnd.unilang:whit.html>whit</a></b>.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1602</b>: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Hamlet" class="extiw" title="s:Hamlet"><a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>Hamlet</a></a></i>, act V scene 2
<dl><dd><i>Not a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:whit.html>whit</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1917</b>, <i>Incident</i> by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Countee_Cullen" class="extiw" title="w:Countee Cullen">Countee Cullen</a>
<dl><dd>Now I <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> eight and very small, \ And he <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> no <b><a href = vnd.unilang:whit.html>whit</a></b> bigger \ And so I smiled, but he poked out \ His tongue, and called <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a>, 'Nigger.'</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">smallest part imaginable</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">bit</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">iota</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">jot</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">scrap</span></li>
<li>See also Thesaurus:modicum.</li></ul>

***whiting.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a> (78044)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">white</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ing</i>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">whitings</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A fine white chalk used in paints, putty, whitewash etc.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">whitening</span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms hyponym"><span class="defdate">Hyponyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">French white</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">Paris white</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">Spanish white</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1918</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:hannah.html>Hannah</a> Teresa Rowley, ‎Mrs. <a href = vnd.unilang:helen.html>Helen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:louise.html>Louise</a> (Wales) Farrell, <i>Principles of Chemistry Applied to the Household</i>
<dl><dd>Precipitated calcium carbonate, a very fine powdery form, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used as a basis for many tooth powders and pastes. As <b><a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></b> it finds a wide use in cleaning metals of their tarnishes.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">white</i></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:242px;"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Merlangius_merlangus.jpg/240px-Merlangius_merlangus.jpg" decoding="async" width="240" height="89" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Merlangius_merlangus.jpg/360px-Merlangius_merlangus.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Merlangius_merlangus.jpg/480px-Merlangius_merlangus.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1190" data-file-height="440" />  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"></div>a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></b> (<i>Merlangius merlangus</i>)</div></div></div>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">whityng</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">whytyng</i>, perhaps an alteration of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">hwītling</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, remodelled after <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">white</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ing</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">diminutive suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to the colour white. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wijting</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">hvítingr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a <a href = vnd.unilang:kind.html>kind</a> of whale</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">whitings</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A fish, <i>Merlangius merlangus</i>, similar to cod, found in the North Atlantic; <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_whiting" class="extiw" title="w:English whiting">English <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></a> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">US</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li>Any fish of many species that resemble <i>Merlangius merlangus</i>:
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of several marine fish found in North American coastal waters, including hakes (genus <i>Merluccius</i>), especially <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Merluccius_bilinearis" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Merluccius bilinearis"><i>Merluccius bilinearis</i></a></span> (the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/silver_hake" class="extiw" title="w:silver hake">silver <a href = vnd.unilang:haken.html>hake</a></a>).</li>
<li>Any of the species of <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Sillaginidae" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Sillaginidae">Sillaginidae</a></span> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/smelt-whiting" class="extiw" title="w:smelt-whiting">smelt-whitings</a>) inhabiting Indo-Pacific marine coasts, many of which are commercially important whitefish.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Canada" class="extiw" title="w:Canada">Canada</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Alaska pollock (<i>Gadus chalcogrammus</i>, syn. <i>Theragra chalcogramma</i>).</li>
<li>A blue <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a> (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Micromesistius_poutassou" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Micromesistius poutassou"><i>Micromesistius poutassou</i></a></span>), a marine fish of the Northern Hemisphere.</li>
<li>A <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/southern_blue_whiting" class="extiw" title="w:southern blue whiting">southern blue <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></a> (<span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Micromesistius_australis" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Micromesistius australis"><i>Micromesistius australis</i></a></span>), a marine fish of the Southern Hemisphere.</li>
<li><span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Menticirrhus_americanus" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Menticirrhus americanus"><i>Menticirrhus americanus</i></a></span> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Carolina_whiting" class="extiw" title="w:Carolina whiting">Carolina <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/king_whiting" class="extiw" title="w:king whiting">king <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/southern_kingcroaker" class="extiw" title="w:southern kingcroaker">southern kingcroaker</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/southern_kingfish" class="extiw" title="w:southern kingfish">southern kingfish</a>) found along the Atlantic and Gulf Coasts of the United States.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/India" class="extiw" title="w:India">India</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any of the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/smelt-whiting" class="extiw" title="w:smelt-whiting">smelt-whitings</a>, of the family <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Sillaginidae" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Sillaginidae">Sillaginidae</a></span>, including <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Japanese_whiting" class="extiw" title="w:Japanese whiting">Japanese <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></a>, King George <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/northern_whiting" class="extiw" title="w:northern whiting">northern <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></a>, sand <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/school_whiting" class="extiw" title="w:school whiting">school <a href = vnd.unilang:whiting.html>whiting</a></a>.</li></ol></li></ol>
</body>

***whoosh.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:whoosh.html>whoosh</a> (62241)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whoosh.html>whoosh</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">whooshes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A breathy sound like that of an object passing at high speed.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b>,  John Branch,  “Snow Fall : The Avalanche at <a href = vnd.unilang:tunnel.html>Tunnel</a> Creek”, in  <cite>New York Time</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.nytimes.com/projects/2012/snow-fall/?smid=fb-nytimesamp;WT.z_sma=SP_SNT_20130415/?part=tunnel-creek">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>The snow burst through the trees with no warning but a last-second <b><a href = vnd.unilang:whoosh.html>whoosh</a></b> of sound, a two-story wall of white and Chris Rudolph’s piercing cry: “Avalanche! Elyse!”</dd></dl></li>
<li>"I love <a href = vnd.unilang:deadlines.html>deadlines</a>. I like the <b>whooshing</b> sound they make as they fly by." —Douglas Adams</li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whoosh.html>whoosh</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">whooshes</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">whooshing</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">whooshed</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To make a breathy sound like a <a href = vnd.unilang:whoosh.html>whoosh</a>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:whoosh.html>whoosh</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sarcastic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Indicating that somebody <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> missed the point (i.e. it <a href = vnd.unilang:went.html>went</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> their head).</span></li></ol>
</body>

***wick.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a> (24320)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:weke.html>weke</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wicke</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wēoce</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*weukan</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flax bundle, <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weg-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to weave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">wjok</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">wjuk</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wiek.html>wiek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wing; propeller, blade; <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Wieche</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wisp; <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicks.html>wicks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A bundle, twist, braid, or woven strip of cord, fabric, fibre/fiber, or other porous material in a candle, oil <a href = vnd.unilang:lamp.html>lamp</a>, kerosene heater, or the like, that draws up liquid fuel, such as melted tallow, wax, or the oil, delivering it to the base of the flame for conversion to gases and burning; any other length of material burned for illumination in small successive portions.
<dl><dd><i>Trim the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> fairly short, so that the flame does not smoke.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Edmund Spenser and provide title, author’s full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>But true it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, that when the oil <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> spent / The light goes out, and <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> thrown away.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Any piece of porous material that conveys liquid by capillary action, such as a strip of gauze placed in a wound to serve as a drain.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">curling</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A narrow opening in the field, flanked by other players' stones.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">curling</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A shot where the played stone touches a stationary stone just enough that the played stone changes direction.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> euphemistic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The <a href = vnd.unilang:penis.html>penis</a>.
<ul><li><b>2008</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:marcus.html>Marcus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>Van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:heller.html>Heller</a>, <i>Nest of Vixens</i>, →ISBN, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.ca/books?id=CG7a6LBMs4kCamp;dq=%22his+wick%22+%22stone+stiff%22amp;q=%22His+wick+was+stone+stiff%22v=snippetamp;q=%22His%20wick%20was%20stone%20stiff%22amp;f=false">p. 17</a>:
<dl><dd>His <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> stone stiff.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2009</b>, Ira Robbins, <i>Kick It Till It <a href = vnd.unilang:breaks.html>Breaks</a></i>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Trouser_Press" class="extiw" title="w:Trouser Press">Trouser Press</a>, →ISBN, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.ca/books?id=j5vOrRdUG4wCamp;dq=sucked+%22his+wick%22+subject%3A%22fiction%22amp;q=%22his+wick%22v=snippetamp;q=%22his%20wick%22amp;f=false">p. 130</a>:
<dl><dd>Her laugh wasn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> cruel in tone, but it cut through Husk like a <a href = vnd.unilang:scalpel.html>scalpel</a>, withering his <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> further.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">candlewick</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">get on someone's <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicks.html>wicks</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">wicking</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">wicked</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To convey or draw off (liquid) by capillary action.
<dl><dd><i>The fabric <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wicks.html>wicks</a></b> perspiration away from the body.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> of a liquid</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To traverse (i.e. be conveyed by capillary action) through a <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a> or other porous material, as water through a sponge. Usually followed by <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">through</i>.
<dl><dd><i>The moisture slowly <b>wicked</b> through the wood.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">curling</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To strike (a stone) obliquely; to strike (a stationary stone) just enough that the played stone changes direction.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From earlier <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:wik.html>wik</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">wich</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">village, <a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>hamlet</a>, town</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wīc</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">dwelling place, abode</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; Germanic borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vīcus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">village, estate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (see <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">vicinity</i>). It <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> to mean “dairy farm” around the 13th or 14th century; for instance, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">Gatwick</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Goat-farm</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">wîch</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">wih</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">village</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Weichbild</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">municipal area</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijk.html>wijk</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">quarter, district</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Frisian" class="extiw" title="w:Old Frisian">Old Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ofs"><a href = vnd.unilang:wik.html>wik</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">wic</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">village</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, as well as <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">οἶκος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oîkos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">eco-</i>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">vicus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicks.html>wicks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li class="senseid" id="English-village"> <span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> clean up<sup class="plainlinks">(<a class="external text" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/w/index.php?title=Wiktionary:Requests_for_cleanupamp;action=editamp;section=newamp;preloadtitle=%5B%5Bwick%5D%5D">+</a>)</sup> this sense?)</span> <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A village; <a href = vnd.unilang:hamlet.html>hamlet</a>; castle; dwelling; street; creek; bay; harbour; a place of work, jurisdiction, or exercise of authority.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/East_Anglia" class="extiw" title="w:East Anglia">East Anglia</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Essex" class="extiw" title="w:Essex">Essex</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A farm, especially a dairy farm.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>Present in compounds (meaning “village”, “jurisdiction”, or “harbour”), as <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-wick</i>, such as bailiwick, sheriffwick, Warwick, Greenwick, Gatwick, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Southwick,_Hampshire" class="extiw" title="w:Southwick, Hampshire">Southwick</a>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">Hampton <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>Wick</a></span> etc., also <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-wich</i>.</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">cwic</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">alive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; similar to an archaic meaning of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">quick</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">endowed with life; having a high degree of vigor, energy, or activity</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">quicken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">come to life</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">wicker</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">wickest</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yorkshire" class="extiw" title="w:Yorkshire">Yorkshire</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Alive; lively; full of life; active; bustling; nimble; quick.
<dl><dd><i>as <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> as an eel</i></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>T</a>' <b>wickest</b> young chap at ivver <a href = vnd.unilang:ah.html>Ah</a> seen.</i></dd>
<dd><i>He's a strange <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:bairn.html>bairn</a> alus runnin' aboot.</i></dd>
<dd><i>I'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> skin ye <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b>!</i> (skin you alive)</dd>
<dd><i>I thowt they <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> dead last back end but they're <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> enif noo.</i></dd>
<dd><i>"Are you afraid of going across the churchyard in the dark?" "<a href = vnd.unilang:lor.html>Lor</a>' bless yer noä miss! It isn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> dead <a href = vnd.unilang:uns.html>uns</a> I'm scar'd on, it's <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:uns.html>uns</a>."</i></dd>
<dd><i>I'<a href = vnd.unilang:ll.html>ll</a> swop wi' him my poor dead horse for his <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b>.</i> — <i>Ballads and <a href = vnd.unilang:songs.html>Songs</a> of the Peasantry of England</i>, page 210</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly Yorkshire</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> (Of inanimate <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a>) resistant to being put to use, stiff, stubborn (as for example a rope or a screw).</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">wicken</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yorkshire" class="extiw" title="w:Yorkshire">Yorkshire</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Liveliness; life.
<dl><dd><i>I niver <a href = vnd.unilang:knew.html>knew</a> such an a thing afore in all my <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b>.</i> — Ashby, 12 July 1875</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yorkshire" class="extiw" title="w:Yorkshire">Yorkshire</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The growing part of a plant nearest to the roots.
<dl><dd><i>Fed close? Why, it's eaten into <a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a>' hard <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b>.</i> (<a href = vnd.unilang:spoken.html>spoken</a> of a pasture which <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> fed very close)</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yorkshire" class="extiw" title="w:Yorkshire">Yorkshire</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> horticulture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>  (Usually plural) The parts of weed roots that remain viable in the ground after inadequate digging prior to cultivation.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain" class="extiw" title="w:Great Britain">Britain</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> dialect<span class="ib-comma">,</span> chiefly <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yorkshire" class="extiw" title="w:Yorkshire">Yorkshire</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A maggot.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology 4</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non"><a href = vnd.unilang:vik.html>vik</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicks.html>wicks</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">now  dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A corner of the mouth or eye.
<ul><li><b>1969</b>, Vladimir Nabokov, <i>Ada or Ardor</i>, Penguin 2011, p. 57:
<dl><dd>She considered him. A fiery droplet in the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wick.html>wick</a></b> of her mouth considered him.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***wiebelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wiebelen.html>wiebelen</a> (28948)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">*wippelen</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wippen.html>wippen</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-elen</i>, influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wiegelen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wipperen</i>, etc. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">wobble</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">wabbeln</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">wabbeln</i>.
</p>
